### Multiplication on the standard finite sets

<pre class="Agda"><a id="mul-Finᵉ"></a><a id="10477" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10477" class="Function">mul-Finᵉ</a> <a id="10486" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="10490" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10491" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10491" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="10494" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10496" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="10498" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10500" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10502" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="10507" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10491" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="10510" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10512" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="10517" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10491" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="10520" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10522" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="10527" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10491" class="Bound">kᵉ</a>
<a id="10530" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10477" class="Function">mul-Finᵉ</a> <a id="10539" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10540" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10548" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10548" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="10550" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10552" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10552" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="10555" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10555" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="10558" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="10562" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1542" class="Function">mod-succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10574" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10548" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="10577" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="10579" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7340" class="Function">nat-Finᵉ</a> <a id="10588" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10589" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10597" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10548" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="10599" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10601" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10552" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="10603" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10605" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1390" class="Function Operator">*ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10609" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10610" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7340" class="Function">nat-Finᵉ</a> <a id="10619" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10620" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="10628" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10548" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="10630" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10632" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10555" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="10634" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="mul-Fin&#39;ᵉ"></a><a id="10638" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10638" class="Function">mul-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="10648" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="10652" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10653" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10653" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="10656" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10658" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="10660" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10662" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10664" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="10669" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10653" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="10672" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10674" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="10679" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10653" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="10682" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10684" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="10689" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10653" class="Bound">kᵉ</a>
<a id="10692" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10638" class="Function">mul-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="10702" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10702" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="10705" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10705" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="10708" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10708" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="10711" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10713" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10477" class="Function">mul-Finᵉ</a> <a id="10722" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10702" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="10725" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10708" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="10728" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10705" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>

<a id="ap-mul-Finᵉ"></a><a id="10732" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10732" class="Function">ap-mul-Finᵉ</a> <a id="10744" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="10748" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10749" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10749" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="10752" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10754" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="10756" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10758" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10759" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10759" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="10762" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10762" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="10765" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10765" class="Bound">x&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="10769" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10769" class="Bound">y&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="10773" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10775" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="10780" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10749" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="10782" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10784" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="10788" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10759" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="10791" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="10794" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10765" class="Bound">x&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="10798" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10800"       <a id="14759" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="14761" class="Argument">x1ᵉ</a> <a id="14765" class="Symbol">=</a>
        <a id="14775" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#834" class="Function">add-ℕᵉ</a>
          <a id="14792" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14794" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7340" class="Function">nat-Finᵉ</a> <a id="14803" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14804" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="14812" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14562" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="14814" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14816" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14817" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10051" class="Function">neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="14826" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14827" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="14835" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14562" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="14837" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14839" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14565" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="14841" class="Symbol">))</a>
          <a id="14854" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14856" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7340" class="Function">nat-Finᵉ</a> <a id="14865" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14866" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="14874" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14562" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="14876" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14878" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14565" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="14880" class="Symbol">)}</a>
      <a id="14889" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="14891" class="Argument">x2ᵉ</a> <a id="14895" class="Symbol">=</a>

        <a id="15156" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15158" href="elementary-number-theory.distance-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1282" class="Function">dist-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15166" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15167" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7340" class="Function">nat-Finᵉ</a> <a id="15176" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15177" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15185" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14562" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="15187" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15189" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14565" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="15191" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15193" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15194" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15202" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14562" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="15204" class="Symbol">))</a>

      <a id="15278" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15280" href="elementary-number-theory.distance-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7294" class="Function">is-difference-dist-ℕ&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="15303" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15304" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7340" class="Function">nat-Finᵉ</a> <a id="15313" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15314" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15322" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14562" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="15324" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15326" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14565" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="15328" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15330" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15331" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15339" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14562" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="15341" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="15351" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15353" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7960" class="Function">upper-bound-nat-Finᵉ</a> <a id="15374" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15375" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15383" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14562" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="15385" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15387" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15388" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#473" class="InductiveConstructor">inlᵉ</a> <a id="15393" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14565" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="15395" class="Symbol">)))</a>
      <a id="15405" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15407" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="Function">cong-zero-ℕ&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="15421" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15422" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15430" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14562" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="15432" class="Symbol">)))</a>

<a id="right-inverse-law-add-Finᵉ"></a><a id="15437" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15437" class="Function">right-inverse-law-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="15464" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="15468" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15469" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15469" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="15472" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15474" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="15476" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15478" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15479" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15479" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="15482" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15484" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="15489" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15490" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15498" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15469" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="15500" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="15503" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="15507" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6155" class="Function">is-zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="15520" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15521" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15529" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15469" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="15531" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15533" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15534" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6603" class="Function">add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="15543" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15544" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15552" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15469" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="15554" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15556" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15479" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="15559" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15560" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10051" class="Function">neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="15569" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15570" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15578" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15469" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="15580" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15582" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15479" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="15584" class="Symbol">))</a>
<a id="15587" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15437" class="Function">right-inverse-law-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="15614" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15614" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="15617" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15617" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="15620" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="15624" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15626" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11209" class="Function">commutative-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="15647" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15648" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15656" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15614" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="15658" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15660" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15617" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="15663" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15664" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10051" class="Function">neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="15673" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15674" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15682" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15614" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="15684" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15686" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15617" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="15688" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="15691" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
  <a id="15696" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15698" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14387" class="Function">left-inverse-law-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="15724" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15614" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="15727" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15617" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="15729" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### The successor function on a standard finite set adds one

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-add-one-succ-Fin&#39;ᵉ"></a><a id="15806" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15806" class="Function">is-add-one-succ-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="15828" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="15832" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15833" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15833" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="15836" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15838" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="15840" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15842" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15843" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15843" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="15846" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15848" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="15853" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15854" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15862" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15833" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="15864" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="15867" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="15871" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6721" class="Function">succ-Finᵉ</a> <a id="15881" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15882" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15890" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15833" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="15892" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15894" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15843" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="15897" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="15900" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6603" class="Function">add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="15909" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15910" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="15918" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15833" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="15920" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15922" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15843" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="15925" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15926" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10455" class="Function">one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="15935" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15833" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="15937" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="16028" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16030" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions%25E1%25B5%2589.html#735" class="Function">apᵉ</a> <a id="16034" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16035" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6721" class="Function">succ-Finᵉ</a> <a id="16045" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16046" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16054" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16055" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16063" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16017" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="16065" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="16069" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16070" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="16075" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16076" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4903" class="Function">is-section-nat-Finᵉ</a> <a id="16096" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16097" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16105" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16017" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="16107" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16109" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16021" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="16111" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="16115" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>

      <a id="16225" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16227" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="16232" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16233" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10847" class="Function">is-one-nat-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="16253" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16254" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16262" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16017" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="16264" class="Symbol">)))))</a>

### Successor laws for addition on Fin k

  <a id="16765" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16767" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions%25E1%25B5%2589.html#735" class="Function">apᵉ</a> <a id="16771" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16772" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6603" class="Function">add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="16781" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16782" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16790" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16751" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="16792" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16794" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16755" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="16796" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16798" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16799" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15806" class="Function">is-add-one-succ-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="16821" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16751" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="16824" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16758" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="16826" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="16829" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
  <a id="16834" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16836" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16838" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="16843" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16844" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11452" class="Function">associative-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="16865" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16866" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16874" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16751" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="16876" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16878" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16755" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="16881" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16758" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="16884" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16885" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10455" class="Function">one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="16894" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16751" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="16896" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="16900" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
    <a id="16907" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16909" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="16914" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16915" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15806" class="Function">is-add-one-succ-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="16937" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16751" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="16940" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16941" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6603" class="Function">add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="16950" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16951" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="16959" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16751" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="16961" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16963" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16755" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="16966" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16758" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="16968" class="Symbol">))))</a>

    <a id="17248" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17250" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions%25E1%25B5%2589.html#735" class="Function">apᵉ</a> <a id="17254" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17255" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6721" class="Function">succ-Finᵉ</a> <a id="17265" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17135" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="17267" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17269" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17270" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11209" class="Function">commutative-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="17291" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17135" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="17294" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17141" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="17297" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17138" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="17299" class="Symbol">)))</a>

  <a id="24131" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24133" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24135" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#21471" class="Function">left-distributive-mul-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="24166" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24060" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="24169" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24069" class="Bound">zᵉ</a> <a id="24172" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24063" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="24175" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24066" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="24177" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24179" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
    <a id="24186" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24188" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6854" class="Function">ap-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="24200" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24060" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="24203" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24204" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#19238" class="Function">commutative-mul-Finᵉ</a> <a id="24225" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24060" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="24228" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24069" class="Bound">zᵉ</a> <a id="24231" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24063" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="24233" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24235" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24236" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#19238" class="Function">commutative-mul-Finᵉ</a> <a id="24257" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24060" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="24260" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24069" class="Bound">zᵉ</a> <a id="24263" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24066" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="24265" class="Symbol">)))</a>
</pre>
## Properties

### Addition on `Fin k` is a binary equivalence

<pre class="Agda"><a id="add-add-neg-Finᵉ"></a><a id="24346" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24346" class="Function">add-add-neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="24363" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="24367" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24368" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24368" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="24371" id="24397" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6603" class="Function">add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="24406" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24368" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="24409" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24378" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="24412" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24413"   <a id="27007" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27008" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27008" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="27011" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27013" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="27015" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27017" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27018" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27018" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="27021" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27023" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="27028" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27008" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="27030" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27032" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27034" href="foundation-core.injective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1002" class="Function">is-injectiveᵉ</a> <a id="27048" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27049" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6762" class="Function">add-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="27059" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27008" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="27062" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27018" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="27064" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="27066" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26980" class="Function">is-injective-add-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="27089" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27089" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="27092" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27092" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="27095" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27096" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27096" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="27098" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27100" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27101" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27101" class="Bound">zᵉ</a><a id="27103" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27105" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27105" class="Bound">pᵉ</a> <a id="27108" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="27112" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26729" class="Function">is-injective-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="27134" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27089" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="27137" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27092" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
    <a id="27144" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27146" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11209" class="Function">commutative-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="27167" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27089" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="27170" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27092" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="27173" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27096" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="27176" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a> <a id="27179" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27180" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27105" class="Bound">pᵉ</a> <a id="27183" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a> <a id="27186" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11209" class="Function">commutative-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="27207" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27089" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="27210" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27101" class="Bound">zᵉ</a> <a id="27213" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#27092" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="27215" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>

        <a id="27631" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27633" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="27635" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a>

### The negative of `-1` is `1`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-one-neg-neg-one-Finᵉ"></a><a id="28078" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28078" class="Function">is-one-neg-neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28102" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="28106" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28107" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28107" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="28110" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28112" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="28114" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28116" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28118" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10549" class="Function">is-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28130" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28131" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="28139" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28107" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28141" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28143" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28144" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10051" class="Function">neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28153" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28154" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="28162" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28107" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28164" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28166" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28167" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2463" class="Function">neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28180" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28107" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28182" class="Symbol">))</a>
<a id="28185" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28078" class="Function">is-one-neg-neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28209" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28209" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="28212" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="28216" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3601" class="Function">eq-mod-succ-cong-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="28236" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28209" class="Bound">kᵉ</a>
    <a id="28243" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28245" href="elementary-number-theory.distance-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1282" class="Function">dist-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="28253" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28209" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="28256" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28257" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="28265" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28209" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28267" class="Symbol">))</a>
    <a id="28274" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28276" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#862" class="Function">1ᵉ</a><a id="28278" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="28284" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28286" href="elementary-number-theory.congruence-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2360" class="Function">cong-identification-ℕᵉ</a>
      <a id="28315" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28317" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="28325" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28209" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28327" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="28335" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28337" href="elementary-number-theory.distance-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2131" class="Function">is-one-dist-succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="28357" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28209" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28359" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### The negative of `1` is `-1`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-neg-one-neg-one-Finᵉ"></a><a id="28408" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28408" class="Function">is-neg-one-neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28432" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="28436" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28437" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28437" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="28440" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28442" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="28444" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28446" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28448" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10051" class="Function">neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28457" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28458" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="28466" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28437" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28468" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28470" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28471" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10455" class="Function">one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28480" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28437" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28482" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28484" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="28487" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28488" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2463" class="Function">neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28501" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28437" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28503" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="28505" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28408" class="Function">is-neg-one-neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28529" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28529" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="28532" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="28536" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26729" class="Function">is-injective-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28558" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28559" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="28567" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28529" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28569" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28571" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28572" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10455" class="Function">one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28581" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28529" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28583" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="28589" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28591" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28593" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15437" class="Function">right-inverse-law-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28620" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28529" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="28623" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28624" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10455" class="Function">one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28633" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28529" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28635" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="28638" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
      <a id="28647" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28649" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28651" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="28656" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28657" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14387" class="Function">left-inverse-law-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28683" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28529" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="28686" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28687" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2463" class="Function">neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28700" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28529" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28702" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="28706" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
        <a id="28717" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28719" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions%25E1%25B5%2589.html#735" class="Function">apᵉ</a> <a id="28723" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28724" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6762" class="Function">add-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="28734" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28735" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="28743" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28529" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28745" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28747" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28748" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2463" class="Function">neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28761" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28529" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28763" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="28766" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28767" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28078" class="Function">is-one-neg-neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28791" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28529" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28793" class="Symbol">))))</a>

### The predecessor function adds `-1`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-add-neg-one-pred-Fin&#39;ᵉ"></a><a id="28851" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28851" class="Function">is-add-neg-one-pred-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="28877" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="28881" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28882" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28882" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="28885" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28887" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="28889" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28891" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28892" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28892" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="28895" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28897" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="28902" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28903" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="28911" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28882" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28913" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="28916" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="28920" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13064" class="Function">pred-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28930" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28931" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="28939" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28882" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28941" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28943" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28892" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="28946" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="28949" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6603" class="Function">add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28958" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28959" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="28967" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28882" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28969" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28971" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28892" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="28974" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28975" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2463" class="Function">neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="28988" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28882" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="28990" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="28992" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28851" class="Function">is-add-neg-one-pred-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="29018" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29018" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="29021" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29021" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="29024" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="29028" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12197" class="Function">is-injective-succ-Finᵉ</a>
    <a id="29055" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29057" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="29065" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29018" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29067" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="29073" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29075" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29077" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13832" class="Function">is-section-pred-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29098" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29099" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="29107" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29018" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29109" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29111" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29021" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="29113" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29115" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
      <a id="29124" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29126" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29128" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29130" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29132" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="29137" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29138" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13520" class="Function">right-unit-law-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29162" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29018" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="29165" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29021" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="29167" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="29170" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
            <a id="29185" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29187" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions%25E1%25B5%2589.html#735" class="Function">apᵉ</a>
              <a id="29205" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29207" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6603" class="Function">add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29216" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29217" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="29225" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29018" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29227" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29229" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29021" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="29231" class="Symbol">)</a>
              <a id="29247" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29249" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a>
                <a id="29270" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29272" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29274" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions%25E1%25B5%2589.html#735" class="Function">apᵉ</a>
                    <a id="29298" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29300" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6762" class="Function">add-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="29310" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29311" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="29319" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29018" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29321" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29323" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29324" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10455" class="Function">one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29333" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29018" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29335" class="Symbol">))</a>
                    <a id="29358" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29360" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="29365" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29366" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28408" class="Function">is-neg-one-neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29390" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29018" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29392" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="29396" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
                  <a id="29417" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29419" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14387" class="Function">left-inverse-law-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29445" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29018" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="29448" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29449" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10455" class="Function">one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29458" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29018" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29460" class="Symbol">))))))</a> <a id="29467" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
          <a id="29480" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29482" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a>
            <a id="29499" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29501" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11452" class="Function">associative-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29522" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29523" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="29531" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29018" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29533" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29535" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29021" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="29538" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29539" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2463" class="Function">neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29552" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29018" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29554" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29556" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29557" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10455" class="Function">one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29566" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29018" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29568" class="Symbol">))))</a> <a id="29573" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
        <a id="29584" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29586" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="29591" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29592" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15806" class="Function">is-add-one-succ-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="29614" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29018" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="29617" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29618" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6603" class="Function">add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29627" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29628" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="29636" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29018" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29638" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29640" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29021" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="29643" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29644" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2463" class="Function">neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29657" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29018" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29659" class="Symbol">))))))</a>

<a id="is-add-neg-one-pred-Finᵉ"></a><a id="29667" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29667" class="Function">is-add-neg-one-pred-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29692" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="29696" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29697" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29697" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="29700" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29702" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="29704" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29706" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29707" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29707" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="29710" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29712" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="29717" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29718" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="29726" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29697" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29728" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="29731" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="29735" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13064" class="Function">pred-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29745" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29746" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="29754" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29697" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29756" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29758" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29707" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="29761" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="29764" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6603" class="Function">add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29773" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29774" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="29782" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29697" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29784" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29786" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29787" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2463" class="Function">neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29800" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29697" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29802" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29804" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29707" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
<a id="29807" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29667" class="Function">is-add-neg-one-pred-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29832" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29832" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="29835" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29835" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="29838" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="29842" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29844" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28851" class="Function">is-add-neg-one-pred-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="29870" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29832" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="29873" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29835" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="29875" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29877" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
  <a id="29882" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29884" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11209" class="Function">commutative-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29905" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29906" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="29914" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29832" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29916" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29918" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29835" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="29921" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29922" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2463" class="Function">neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="29935" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29832" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="29937" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### `neg-Fin` multiplies by `-1`

          <a id="30872" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30874" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#19662" class="Function">left-unit-law-mul-Finᵉ</a> <a id="30897" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#30149" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="30900" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#30152" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="30902" class="Symbol">))))</a>

<a id="is-mul-neg-one-neg-Fin&#39;ᵉ"></a><a id="30908" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#30908" class="Function">is-mul-neg-one-neg-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="30933" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="30937" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30938" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#30938" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="30941" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30943" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="30945" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30947" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30948" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#30948" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="30951" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30953" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="30958" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30959" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="30967" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#30938" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="30969" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="30972" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="30976" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10051" class="Function">neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="30985" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30986" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="30994" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#30938" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="30996" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30998" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#30948" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="31001" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="31004" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10477" class="Function">mul-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31013" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31014" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="31022" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#30938" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="31024" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31026" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#30948" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="31029" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31030" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2463" class="Function">neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31043" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#30938" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="31045" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="31047" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#30908" class="Function">is-mul-neg-one-neg-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="31072" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31072" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="31075" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31075" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="31078" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="31082" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29987" class="Function">is-mul-neg-one-neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31106" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31072" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="31109" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31075" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="31112" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a> <a id="31115" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#19238" class="Function">commutative-mul-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31136" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31137" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="31145" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31072" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="31147" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31149" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31150" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2463" class="Function">neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31163" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31072" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="31165" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31167" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31075" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
</pre>
### The negative of `0` is `0`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="neg-zero-Finᵉ"></a><a id="31215" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31215" class="Function">neg-zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31229" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31231" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31232" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31232" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="31235" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31237" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="31239" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31241" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31243" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10051" class="Function">neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31252" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31253" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="31261" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31232" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="31263" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31265" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31266" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6036" class="Function">zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31276" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31232" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="31278" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31280" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="31283" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6036" class="Function">zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31293" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31232" class="Bound">kᵉ</a>
<a id="31296" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31215" class="Function">neg-zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31310" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31310" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="31313" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="31317" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="31319" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="31324" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31325" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14150" class="Function">left-unit-law-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31348" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31310" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="31351" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31352" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10051" class="Function">neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31361" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31362" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="31370" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31310" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="31372" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31374" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31375" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6036" class="Function">zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31385" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31310" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="31387" class="Symbol">))))</a> <a id="31392" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
  <a id="31397" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="31399" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15437" class="Function">right-inverse-law-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31426" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31310" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="31429" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31430" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6036" class="Function">zero-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31440" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31310" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="31442" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### The negative of a successor is the predecessor of the negative

<pre class="Agda"><a id="neg-succ-Finᵉ"></a><a id="31526" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31526" class="Function">neg-succ-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31540" class="Symbol">:</a>

<a id="31634" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31526" class="Function">neg-succ-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31648" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31649" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="31657" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31657" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="31659" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31661" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31661" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="31664" class="Symbol">=</a>
