    <a id="31814" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="31816" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="31818" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#21471" class="Function">left-distributive-mul-add-Finᵉ</a>
        <a id="31857" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="31859" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="31867" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31657" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="31869" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="31879" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="31881" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2463" class="Function">neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31894" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31657" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="31896" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="31906" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="31908" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31661" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="31910" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="31920" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="31922" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10455" class="Function">one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="31931" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31657" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="31933" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="31936" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
      <a id="31945" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="31947" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="31949" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6854" class="Function">ap-add-Finᵉ</a>
          <a id="31971" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="31973" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="31981" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31657" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="31983" class="Symbol">)</a>
          <a id="31995" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="31997" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="32002" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32003" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29987" class="Function">is-mul-neg-one-neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="32027" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31657" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="32030" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31661" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="32032" class="Symbol">))</a>
          <a id="32045" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="32047" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="32049" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="32054" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32055" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29987" class="Function">is-mul-neg-one-neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="32079" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31657" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="32082" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32083" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10455" class="Function">one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="32092" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31657" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="32094" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="32098" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
            <a id="32113" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="32115" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28408" class="Function">is-neg-one-neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="32139" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31657" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="32141" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="32145" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
        <a id="32156" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="32158" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="32163" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32164" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28851" class="Function">is-add-neg-one-pred-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="32190" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31657" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="32193" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32194" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10051" class="Function">neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="32203" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32204" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="32212" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31657" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="32214" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32216" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31661" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="32218" class="Symbol">))))))</a>
</pre>
### The negative of a predecessor is the successor of a negative

        <a id="32643" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="32645" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="32653" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#32435" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="32655" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="32665" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="32667" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2463" class="Function">neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="32680" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#32435" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="32682" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="32692" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="32694" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#32439" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="32696" class="Symbol">)</a>

### Taking negatives distributes over addition

<pre class="Agda"><a id="distributive-neg-add-Finᵉ"></a><a id="33076" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33076" class="Function">distributive-neg-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="33102" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="33106" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33107" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33107" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="33110" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33112" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="33114" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33116" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33117" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33117" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="33120" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33120" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="33123" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33125" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="33130" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33107" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="33132" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33134" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="33138" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10051" class="Function">neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="33147" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33107" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="33150" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33151" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6603" class="Function">add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="33160" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33117" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="33166" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33120" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="33168" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33170" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="33173" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6603" class="Function">add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="33182" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33107" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="33185" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33186" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10051" class="Function">neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="33195" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33107" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="33198" id="33203" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10051" class="Function">neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="33212" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33107" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="33215" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33120" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="33217" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="33219" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33076" class="Function">distributive-neg-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="33245" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33246" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="33254" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33254" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="33256" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33258" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33258" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="33261" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33261" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="33264" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="33268" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="33270" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29987" class="Function">is-mul-neg-one-neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="33294" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33254" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="33297" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33298" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6603" class="Function">add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="33307" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33308" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="33316" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33254" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="33318" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33320" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33258" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="33323" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33261" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="33325" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="33328" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
  <a id="33333" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="33335" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="33337" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#21471" class="Function">left-distributive-mul-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="33368" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33369" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="33377" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33254" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="33379" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33381" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33382" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2463" class="Function">neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="33395" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33254" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="33397" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33399" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33258" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="33402" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33261" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="33404" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33406" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
    <a id="33413" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="33415" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a>
      <a id="33426" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="33428" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6854" class="Function">ap-add-Finᵉ</a>
        <a id="33448" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="33450" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="33458" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33254" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="33460" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="33470" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="33472" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29987" class="Function">is-mul-neg-one-neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="33496" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33254" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="33499" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33258" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="33501" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="33511" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="33513" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29987" class="Function">is-mul-neg-one-neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="33537" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33254" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="33540" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#33261" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="33542" class="Symbol">))))</a>
</pre>
### Predecessor laws of addition

  <a id="34185" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="34187" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions%25E1%25B5%2589.html#735" class="Function">apᵉ</a> <a id="34191" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34192" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6603" class="Function">add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="34201" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34202" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="34210" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34171" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="34212" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34214" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34175" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="34216" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34218" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34219" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28851" class="Function">is-add-neg-one-pred-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="34245" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34171" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="34248" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34178" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="34250" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="34253" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
  <a id="34258" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="34260" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="34262" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="34267" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34268" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11452" class="Function">associative-add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="34289" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34290" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="34298" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34171" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="34300" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34302" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34175" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="34305" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34178" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="34308" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34309" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2463" class="Function">neg-one-Finᵉ</a> <a id="34322" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34171" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="34324" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="34328" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>
    <a id="34335" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="34337" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a> <a id="34342" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34343" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28851" class="Function">is-add-neg-one-pred-Fin&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="34369" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34171" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="34372" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34373" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6603" class="Function">add-Finᵉ</a> <a id="34382" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34383" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="34391" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34171" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="34393" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34395" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34175" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="34398" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34178" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="34400" class="Symbol">))))</a>
</pre>
### Negative laws of multiplication

<pre class="Agda"><a id="left-negative-law-mul-Finᵉ"></a><a id="34455" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34455" class="Function">left-negative-law-mul-Finᵉ</a> <a id="34482" class="Symbol">:</a>

  <a id="34518" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10477" class="Function">mul-Finᵉ</a> <a id="34527" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34487" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="34530" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34531" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10051" class="Function">neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="34540" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34487" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="34543" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34497" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="34545" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34547" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34500" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="34550" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="34553" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10051" class="Function">neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="34562" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34487" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="34565" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34566" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10477" class="Function">mul-Finᵉ</a> <a id="34575" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34487" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="34578" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34497" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="34581" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34500" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="34583" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="34585" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34455" class="Function">left-negative-law-mul-Finᵉ</a> <a id="34612" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34613" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="34621" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34621" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="34623" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34625" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34625" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="34628" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#34628" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="34631" class="Symbol">=</a>

</pre>
### Successor laws of multiplication

### Predecessor laws of multiplication

<pre class="Agda"><a id="left-predecessor-law-mul-Finᵉ"></a><a id="36218" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#36218" class="Function">left-predecessor-law-mul-Finᵉ</a> <a id="36248" class="Symbol">:</a>

  <a id="36284" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10477" class="Function">mul-Finᵉ</a> <a id="36293" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#36253" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="36296" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36297" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13064" class="Function">pred-Finᵉ</a> <a id="36307"   <a id="36899" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="36901" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions%25E1%25B5%2589.html#735" class="Function">apᵉ</a> <a id="36905" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36906" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10477" class="Function">mul-Finᵉ</a> <a id="36915" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36916" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="36924" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#36885" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="36926" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="36928" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#36889" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="36930" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="36932" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36933" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29667" class="Function">is-add-neg-one-pred-Finᵉ</a> <a id="36958" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#36885" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="36961" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#36892" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="36963" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="36966" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5906" class="Function Operator">∙ᵉ</a>

### Taking negatives is an involution

<pre class="Agda"><a id="neg-neg-Finᵉ"></a><a id="37220" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#37220" class="Function">neg-neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="37233" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="37237" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37238" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#37238" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="37241" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="37243" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="37245" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="37247" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37248" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#37248" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="37251" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="37253" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2093" class="Function">Finᵉ</a> <a id="37258" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#37238" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="37260" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="37262" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="37264" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10051" class="Function">neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="37273" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#37238" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="37276" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37277" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10051" class="Function">neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="37286" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#37238" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="37289" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#37248" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="37291" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="37293" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="37296" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#37248" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
<a id="37299" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#37220" class="Function">neg-neg-Finᵉ</a> <a id="37312" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37313" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#821" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="37321" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#37321" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="37323" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="37325" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#37325" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="37328" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="37332" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="37334" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6276" class="Function">invᵉ</a>

## Properties

### Divisibility is a decidable relation on `ℕ`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-decidable-div-ℕᵉ"></a><a id="38408" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#38408" class="Function">is-decidable-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="38428" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="38430" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38431" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#38431" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="38434" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#38434" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="38437" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="38439" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#783" class="Datatype">ℕᵉ</a><a id="38441" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="38443" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="38445" href="foundation.decidable-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1541" class="Function">is-decidableᵉ</a> <a id="38459" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38460" href="elementary-number-theory.divisibility-natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1704" class="Function">div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="38467" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#38431" class="Bound">dᵉ</a> <a id="38470" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#38434" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="38472" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="38474" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#38408" class="Function">is-decidable-div-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="38494" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers%25E1%25B5%2589.html#806" class="InductiveConstructor">zero-ℕᵉ</a> <a id="38502" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#38502" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="38505" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="38509" href="foundation.decidable-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6739" class="Function">is-decidable-iffᵉ</a>
